protection implementation in GCC is distributed across multiple files with a clear separation between generic/low-level expansion code and target-specific implementations. The feature is controlled by the `-fstack-clash-protection` flag defined in `gcc/common.opt` (lines 3054-3057).\\n\\n### Key Files and Components\\n\\n#### 1. **Generic Stack Clash Expansion (gcc/explow.cc)**\\nThe generic stack clash protection implementation resides in `gcc/explow.cc`. This file contains four critical functions:\\n\\n- **`compute_stack_clash_protection_loop_data()`** (line 1955): Computes parameters for the stack clash probing loop, including rounded allocation size, last address, residual size, and probe interval. This function handles both small allocations (inlined probing) and large allocations (loop-based probing).\\n\\n- **`anti_adjust_stack_and_probe_stack_clash()`** (line 2072): The main function for dynamically allocated stack probing. It handles both:\\n  - Small allocations: Probes inline with simple interval-based probes\\n  - Large allocations: Uses loop-based probing with `emit_stack_clash_protection_probe_loop_start()` and `emit_stack_clash_protection_probe_loop_end()`\\n  - Residual allocations: Additional probing for non-aligned remainder\\n\\n- **`emit_stack_clash_protection_probe_loop_start()`** (line 2014): Emits the initialization and top of the stack clash probing loop, generating labels and comparison logic.\\n\\n- **`emit_stack_clash_protection_probe_loop_end()`** (line 2036): Emits the end of the probing loop with appropriate jump instructions.\\n\\nThese functions are declared in `gcc/explow.h` (lines 73-87).\\n\\n#### 2. **Target Hook Definition (gcc/target.def)**\\nThe generic stack clash mechanism is extended via the target hook `TARGET_STACK_CLASH_PROTECTION_ALLOCA_PROBE_RANGE` (lines 6534-6545). This hook allows targets to define an ABI-specific probing interval that may differ from the generic implementation.\\n\\n#### 3. **Default Target Hook Implementation (gcc/targhooks.cc)**\\nThe default implementation of `default_stack_clash_protection_alloca_probe_range()` is defined at line 2746, returning 0 (no target-specific probing range). This is declared in `gcc/targhooks.h` (line 305).\\n\\n#### 4. **x86_64/i386 Target-Specific Implementation**\\n\\n**Machine Description (gcc/config/i386/i386.md):**\\n- **`allocate_stack` pattern** (line 27766): The define_expand pattern that orchestrates stack allocation with probing for x86 targets\\n- **`allocate_stack_worker_probe` pattern** (line 27756): The actual probing instruction pattern for x86\\n- **`probe_stack` pattern** (line 27797): General probe_stack expansion\\n- **Stack probe instructions** (lines 27818-27838): Low-level probe instructions including `adjust_stack_and_probe` and `probe_stack_range`\\n\\n**i386 Implementation Header (gcc/config/i386/i386-protos.h):**\\n- Declares `ix86_target_stack_probe()` function (line 27) that controls whether x86 uses stack probing\\n\\n**i386 Header (gcc/config/i386/i386.h):**\\n- Contains stack probe related macros and definitions\\n\\n**Main i386 Backend (gcc/config/i386/i386.cc):**\\n- Contains the core x86 backend implementation, including frame setup/teardown and stack clash handling during function prologue/epilogue\\n\\n#### 5. **Compiler Options**\\n\\n**Common Options (gcc/common.opt):**\\n- **`-fstack-clash-protection`** (lines 3054-3057): The main flag that enables stack clash protection across all targets that support it.
